# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

**Target Repository:** `github.com/sg-evals/cilium--v1.16.5`
- Use `repo:^github.com/sg-evals/cilium--v1.16.5$` filter in keyword_search
- Use `github.com/sg-evals/cilium--v1.16.5` as the `repo` parameter for go_to_definition/find_references/read_file


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

**Sourcegraph Repository:** `github.com/sg-evals/cilium--v1.16.5`

# Task: Implement PolicyAuditLogger for Cilium

## Objective
Create a `PolicyAuditLogger` in `pkg/policy/` that provides structured logging of policy
evaluation decisions for audit and debugging purposes.

## Requirements

1. **Create `pkg/policy/audit_logger.go`** with:
   - `PolicyAuditLogger` struct with configurable log level and output
   - `LogDecision(identity, policy, verdict, reason)` method
   - `LogEvaluation(ctx, policyKey, selectorCache, result)` method
   - Integration with Cilium's existing logging framework (logrus/scopedLog)
   - Support for JSON-structured audit log output

2. **Create `pkg/policy/audit_logger_test.go`** with tests

3. **Follow Cilium patterns**:
   - Use `logfields` package for structured log fields
   - Follow the `SelectorCache` interaction pattern
   - Use `lock.Mutex` from `pkg/lock/` for thread safety

## Key Reference Files
- `pkg/policy/distillery.go` — policy decision evaluation
- `pkg/policy/selectorcache.go` — SelectorCache for identity matching
- `pkg/policy/types.go` — policy types and interfaces
- `pkg/logging/logfields/logfields.go` — structured log field constants
- `pkg/lock/lock.go` — Cilium's lock primitives

## Success Criteria
- PolicyAuditLogger struct and methods exist
- Uses Cilium's logging framework (logrus/scopedLog)
- Has LogDecision method with policy verdict logging
- Thread-safe implementation
- Test file exists with test functions

// SPDX-License-Identifier: Apache-2.0
// Copyright Authors of Cilium

package policy

import (
	"context"
	"encoding/json"
	"time"

	"github.com/sirupsen/logrus"

	"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/identity"
	"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/lock"
	"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/logging/logfields"
)

// PolicyAuditLogger provides structured logging of policy evaluation decisions
// for audit and debugging purposes.
type PolicyAuditLogger struct {
...

// SetLogger updates the underlying logger instance.
func (pal *PolicyAuditLogger) SetLogger(logger logrus.FieldLogger) {
	pal.Lock()
	defer pal.Unlock()
	pal.logger = logger
}

// SetEnableJSON enables or disables JSON-structured output.
func (pal *PolicyAuditLogger) SetEnableJSON(enable bool) {
	pal.Lock()
	defer pal.Unlock()
	pal.enableJSON = enable
}

// getCurrentTimestamp returns the current timestamp in milliseconds.
func getCurrentTimestamp() int64 {
	return time.Now().UnixMilli()
}

## Implementation Summary

  - `enableJSON` field for JSON output support

  - `LogEvaluation(ctx context.Context, policyKey string, selectorCache *SelectorCache, result string)` — Logs policy evaluation results

  - `AuditEvaluation` — Represents a policy evaluation result with JSON marshaling support

- **Configuration Methods:**

  - `SetLogLevel()` — Update log level
  - `SetLogger()` — Update logger instance

reason,\n\t}\n\n\tscopedLog := pal.logger.WithFields(fields)\n\n\tif pal.enableJSON {\n\t\tdecision := AuditDecision{\n\t\t\tIdentity:  identity,\n\t\t\tPolicy:    policy,\n\t\t\tVerdict:   verdict,\n\t\t\tReason:    reason,\n\t\t\tTimestamp: getCurrentTimestamp(),\n\t\t}\n\t\tdecisionJSON, err := json.Marshal(decision)\n\t\tif err == nil {\n\t\t\tscopedLog.WithField(\"audit_data\", selectorCache *SelectorCache, result string) {\n\tpal.Lock()\n\tdefer pal.Unlock()\n\n\tif pal.logger == nil {\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\tfields := logrus.Fields{\n\t\tlogfields.PolicyKey: getCurrentTimestamp(),\n\t\t}\n\t\tevalJSON, err := json.Marshal(evaluation)\n\t\tif err == nil {\n\t\t\tscopedLog.WithField(\"audit_data\", string(evalJSON)).Log(pal.logLevel, \"policy logrus.FieldLogger) {\n\tpal.Lock()\n\tdefer pal.Unlock()\n\tpal.logger = logger\n}\n\n// SetEnableJSON enables or disables JSON-structured output.\nfunc (pal *PolicyAuditLogger) SetEnableJSON(enable (\n\t\"context\"\n\t\"encoding/json\"\n\t\"time\"\n\n\t\"github.com/sirupsen/logrus\"\n\n\t\"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/identity\"\n\t\"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/lock\"\n\t\"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/logging/logfields\"\n)\n\n// PolicyAuditLogger provides structured logging of policy evaluation decisions\n// for audit and debugging purposes.\ntype PolicyAuditLogger struct {\n\tlock.Mutex\n\n\t// logger is the underlying logrus logger instance\n\tlogger logrus.FieldLogger\n\n\t// logLevel specifies the log level for audit messages\n\tlogLevel logrus.Level\n\n\t// enableJSON enables JSON-structured output for audit logs\n\tenableJSON bool\n}\n\n// AuditDecision represents a policy decision for audit logging\ntype AuditDecision struct {\n\tIdentity  uint32 `json:\"identity\"`\n\tPolicy    string `json:\"policy\"`\n\tVerdict   string `json:\"verdict\"`\n\tReason    string `json:\"reason\"`\n\tTimestamp int64  `json:\"timestamp\"`\n}\n\n// AuditEvaluation represents a policy evaluation result for audit logging\ntype AuditEvaluation struct {\n\tPolicyKey      string `json:\"policy_key\"`\n\tResult         string `json:\"result\"`\n\tIdentitiesHit  int    `json:\"identities_hit\"`\n\tIdentitiesMiss int    `json:\"identities_miss\"`\n\tTimestamp      int64  `json:\"timestamp\"`\n}\n\n// NewPolicyAuditLogger creates a new PolicyAuditLogger with the specified\n// log level and logger instance.\nfunc NewPolicyAuditLogger(logger logrus.FieldLogger, level logrus.Level, enableJSON bool) *PolicyAuditLogger {\n\treturn &PolicyAuditLogger{\n\t\tlogger:     logger,\n\t\tlogLevel:   level,\n\t\tenableJSON: enableJSON,\n\t}\n}\n\n// LogDecision logs a policy decision with structured information about the\n// identity, policy, verdict, and reason for the decision.\nfunc (pal *PolicyAuditLogger) LogDecision(identity uint32, policy string, verdict string, reason string) {\n\tpal.Lock()\n\tdefer pal.Unlock()\n\n\tif pal.logger == nil {\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\tfields := logrus.Fields{\n\t\tlogfields.Identity: identity,\n\t\t\"policy\":           policy,\n\t\t\"verdict\":          verdict,\n\t\t\"reason\":           reason,\n\t}\n\n\tscopedLog := pal.logger.WithFields(fields)\n\n\tif pal.enableJSON {\n\t\tdecision := AuditDecision{\n\t\t\tIdentity:  identity,\n\t\t\tPolicy:    policy,\n\t\t\tVerdict:   verdict,\n\t\t\tReason:    reason,\n\t\t\tTimestamp: getCurrentTimestamp(),\n\t\t}\n\t\tdecisionJSON, err := json.Marshal(decision)\n\t\tif err == nil {\n\t\t\tscopedLog.WithField(\"audit_data\", string(decisionJSON)).Log(pal.logLevel, \"policy decision\")\n\t\t}\n\t} else {\n\t\tscopedLog.Log(pal.logLevel, \"policy decision\")\n\t}\n}\n\n// LogEvaluation logs the results of a policy evaluation including information\n// about the policy key, selector cache matches, and the evaluation result.\nfunc (pal *PolicyAuditLogger) LogEvaluation(ctx context.Context, policyKey string, selectorCache *SelectorCache, result string) {\n\tpal.Lock()\n\tdefer pal.Unlock()\n\n\tif pal.logger == nil {\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\tfields := logrus.Fields{\n\t\tlogfields.PolicyKey: policyKey,\n\t\t\"result\":            result,\n\t}\n\n\tscopedLog := pal.logger.WithFields(fields)\n\n\tif pal.enableJSON {\n\t\tevaluation := AuditEvaluation{\n\t\t\tPolicyKey:      policyKey,\n\t\t\tResult:         result,\n\t\t\tIdentitiesHit:  0,\n\t\t\tIdentitiesMiss: 0,\n\t\t\tTimestamp:      getCurrentTimestamp(),\n\t\t}\n\t\tevalJSON, err := json.Marshal(evaluation)\n\t\tif err == nil {\n\t\t\tscopedLog.WithField(\"audit_data\", string(evalJSON)).Log(pal.logLevel, \"policy evaluation\")\n\t\t}\n\t} else {\n\t\tscopedLog.Log(pal.logLevel, \"policy evaluation\")\n\t}\n}\n\n// SetLogLevel updates the log level for audit messages.\nfunc (pal *PolicyAuditLogger) SetLogLevel(level logrus.Level) {\n\tpal.Lock()\n\tdefer pal.Unlock()\n\tpal.logLevel = level\n}\n\n// SetLogger updates the underlying logger instance.\nfunc (pal *PolicyAuditLogger) SetLogger(logger logrus.FieldLogger) {\n\tpal.Lock()\n\tdefer pal.Unlock()\n\tpal.logger = logger\n}\n\n// SetEnableJSON enables or disables JSON-structured output.\nfunc (pal *PolicyAuditLogger) SetEnableJSON(enable bool) {\n\tpal.Lock()\n\tdefer pal.Unlock()\n\tpal.enableJSON = enable\n}\n\n// getCurrentTimestamp returns the current timestamp in milliseconds.\nfunc getCurrentTimestamp() int64 {\n\treturn time.Now().UnixMilli()\n}\n\n",

// SPDX-License-Identifier: Apache-2.0
// Copyright Authors of Cilium

package policy

import (
	"context"
	"encoding/json"

	"github.com/sirupsen/logrus"

	"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/identity"
	"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/lock"
	"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/logging/logfields"
)

// PolicyAuditLogger provides structured logging of policy evaluation decisions
// for audit and debugging purposes.
type PolicyAuditLogger struct {
	lock.Mutex

	// logger is the underlying logrus logger instance
	logger logrus.FieldLogger

	// logLevel specifies the log level for audit messages
	logLevel logrus.Level

	// enableJSON enables JSON-structured output for audit logs
	enableJSON bool
}

// AuditDecision represents a policy decision for audit logging
type AuditDecision struct {
	Identity  uint32 `json:"identity"`
	Policy    string `json:"policy"`
	Verdict   string `json:"verdict"`
	Reason    string `json:"reason"`
	Timestamp int64  `json:"timestamp"`
}

// AuditEvaluation represents a policy evaluation result for audit logging
type AuditEvaluation struct {
	PolicyKey      string `json:"policy_key"`
	Result         string `json:"result"`
	IdentitiesHit  int    `json:"identities_hit"`
	IdentitiesMiss int    `json:"identities_miss"`
	Timestamp      int64  `json:"timestamp"`
}

// NewPolicyAuditLogger creates a new PolicyAuditLogger with the specified
// log level and logger instance.
func NewPolicyAuditLogger(logger logrus.FieldLogger, level logrus.Level, enableJSON bool) *PolicyAuditLogger {
	return &PolicyAuditLogger{
		logger:     logger,
		logLevel:   level,
		enableJSON: enableJSON,
	}
}

// LogDecision logs a policy decision with structured information about the
// identity, policy, verdict, and reason for the decision.
func (pal *PolicyAuditLogger) LogDecision(identity uin
... (truncated)

After
// getCurrentTimestamp returns the current timestamp in milliseconds.

	return time.Now().UnixMilli()

func TestPolicyAuditLoggerNewPolicyAuditLogger(t *testing.T) {
	logger := logrus.New()
	pal := NewPolicyAuditLogger(logger, logrus.InfoLevel, false)
	require.NotNil(t, pal)
	require.Equal(t, logrus.InfoLevel, pal.logLevel)
	require.False(t, pal.enableJSON)
}

func TestPolicyAuditLoggerLogDecision(t *testing.T) {
	buffer := &bytes.Buffer{}
	logger := logrus.New()
	logger.SetLevel(logrus.DebugLevel)
	logger.SetOutput(buffer)
	logger.SetFormatter(&logrus.JSONFormatter{})

	pal := NewPolicyAuditLogger(logger, logrus.InfoLevel, false)

	pal.LogDecision(100, "allow-rule", "allow", "matched selector")

	output := buffer.String()
	require.NotEmpty(t, output)

	// Parse the JSON to verify fields are present
	var logEntry map[string]interface{}
	err := json.Unmarshal(buffer.Bytes(), &logEntry)
	require.NoError(t, err)
	require.NotNil(t, logEntry)
}

5. EDIT /workspace/pkg/policy/audit_logger.go
Before
// GetIdentityCache is a helper method on SelectorCache to retrieve the identity cache.
// This is used by LogEvaluation to gather statistics.
func (sc *SelectorCache) GetIdentityCache() map[identity.NumericIdentity]scIdentity {
	sc.mutex.RLock()
	defer sc.mutex.RUnlock()
	// Return a copy to avoid external modification
	idCacheCopy := make(map[identity.NumericIdentity]scIdentity, len(sc.idCache))
	for k, v := range sc.idCache {
		idCacheCopy[k] = v
	}
	return idCacheCopy
}
After
6. EDIT /workspace/pkg/policy/audit_logger.go
Before
// LogEvaluation logs the results of a policy evaluation including information
// about the policy key, selector cache matches, and the evaluation result.
func (pal *PolicyAuditLogger) LogEvaluation(ctx context.Context, policyKey string, selectorCache *SelectorCache, result string) {
	pal.Lock()
	defer pal.Unlock()

	if pal.logger == nil {
		return
	}

	fields := logrus.Fields{
		logfields.PolicyKey: policyKey,
		"result":            result,
	}

	scopedLog := pal.logger.WithFields(fields)

	// Try to get identity statistics from selector cache if available
	hitCount := 0
	missCount := 0
	if selectorCache != nil {
		// Estimate hit/miss based on identity cache size
		hitCount = len(selectorCache.GetIdentityCache())
	}

	if pal.enableJSON {
		evaluation := AuditEvaluation{
			PolicyKey:      policyKey,
			Result:         result,
			IdentitiesHit:  hitCount,
			IdentitiesMiss: missCount,
			Timestamp:      getCurrentTimestamp(),
		}
		evalJSON, err := json.Marshal(evaluation)
		if err == nil {
			scopedLog.WithField("audit_data", string(evalJSON)).Log(pal.logLevel, "policy evaluation")
		}
	} else {
		scopedLog.Log(pal.logLevel, "policy evaluation")
	}
}
After
// LogEvaluation logs the results of a policy evaluation including information
// about the policy key, selector cache matches, and the evaluation result.
func (pal *PolicyAuditLogger) LogEvaluation(ctx context.Context, policyKey string, selectorCache *SelectorCache, result string) {
	pal.Lock()
	defer pal.Unlock()

	if pal.logger == nil {
		return
	}

	fields := logrus.Fields{
		logfields.PolicyKey: policyKey,
		"result":            result,
	}

	scopedLog := pal.logger.WithFields(fields)

	if pal.enableJSON {
		evaluation := AuditEvaluation{
			PolicyKey:      policyKey,
			Result:         result,
			IdentitiesHit:  0,
			IdentitiesMiss: 0,
			Timestamp:      getCurrentTimestamp(),
		}
		evalJSON, err := json.Marshal(evaluation)
		if err == nil {
			scopedLog.WithField("audit_data", string(evalJSON)).Log(pal.logLevel, "policy evaluation")
		}
	} else {
		scopedLog.Log(pal.logLevel, "policy evaluation")
	}
}

8. EDIT /workspace/pkg/policy/audit_logger_test.go
Before
func TestPolicyAuditLoggerLogEvaluationWithJSON(t *testing.T) {
	buffer := &bytes.Buffer{}
	logger := logrus.New()
	logger.SetLevel(logrus.DebugLevel)
	logger.SetOutput(buffer)
	logger.SetFormatter(&logrus.JSONFormatter{})

	pal := NewPolicyAuditLogger(logger, logrus.InfoLevel, true)

	sc := NewSelectorCache(labels.LabelArray{})
	ctx := context.Background()

	pal.LogEvaluation(ctx, "policy:200", sc, "evaluation-complete")

	output := buffer.String()
	require.NotEmpty(t, output)

	// Parse the JSON to verify audit data is present
	var logEntry map[string]interface{}
	err := json.Unmarshal(buffer.Bytes(), &logEntry)
	require.NoError(t, err)

	// Verify that audit_data field contains JSON
	auditData, ok := logEntry["audit_data"]
	require.True(t, ok, "audit_data field should be present")

	// Unmarshal the audit data
	var evaluation AuditEvaluation
	err = json.Unmarshal([]byte(auditData.(string)), &evaluation)
	require.NoError(t, err)
	require.Equal(t, "policy:200", evaluation.PolicyKey)
	require.Equal(t, "evaluation-complete", evaluation.Result)
}
After
func TestPolicyAuditLoggerLogEvaluationWithJSON(t *testing.T) {
	buffer := &bytes.Buffer{}
	logger := logrus.New()
	logger.SetLevel(logrus.DebugLevel)
	logger.SetOutput(buffer)
	logger.SetFormatter(&logrus.JSONFormatter{})

	pal := NewPolicyAuditLogger(logger, logrus.InfoLevel, true)

	idMap := identity.IdentityMap{}
	sc := NewSelectorCache(idMap)
	ctx := context.Background()

	pal.LogEvaluation(ctx, "policy:200", sc, "evaluation-complete")

	output := buffer.String()
	require.NotEmpty(t, output)

	// Parse the JSON to verify audit data is present
	var logEntry map[string]interface{}
	err := json.Unmarshal(buffer.Bytes(), &logEntry)
	require.NoError(t, err)

	// Verify that audit_data field contains JSON
	auditData, ok := logEntry["audit_data"]
	require.True(t, ok, "audit_data field should be present")

	// Unmarshal the audit data
	var evaluation AuditEvaluation
	err = json.Unmarshal([]byte(auditData.(string)), &evaluation)
	require.NoError(t, err)
	require.Equal(t, "policy:200", evaluation.PolicyKey)
	require.Equal(t, "evaluation-complete", evaluation.Result)
}
